permitted by Regulation S-T Rule&nbsp;101 (b)(7): </font><font size="2" face="Wingdings" style="font-size:10.0pt;">o</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Note:
</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Regulation S-T Rule&nbsp;101(b)(7)&nbsp;only
permits the submission in paper of a Form&nbsp;6-K if submitted to furnish a
report or other document that the registrant foreign private issuer must
furnish and make public under the laws of the jurisdiction in which the
registrant is incorporated, domiciled or legally organized (the registrant&#146;s &#147;home
country&#148;), or under the rules&nbsp;of the home country exchange on which the
registrant&#146;s securities are traded, as long as the report or other document is
not a press release, is not required to be and has not been distributed to the
registrant&#146;s security holders, and, if discussing a material event, has already
been the subject of a Form&nbsp;6-K submission or other Commission filing on
EDGAR.</font></p>

<div>

<p align="right" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit 1</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 13.5pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(All amounts expressed in
U.S. dollars unless otherwise noted)</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 13.5pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AGNICO-EAGLE PROVIDES
EXPLORATION UPDATE ON 2009 ACTIVITIES:</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">NEW GOLD DISCOVERY AT
CUBIRO AT PINOS ALTOS</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Toronto (September&nbsp;08,
2009) - <b>Agnico-Eagle Mines Limited</b>
(&#147;Agnico-Eagle&#148; or the &#147;Company&#148;) is pleased to provide an update on its 2009
exploration program.&#160; New discoveries
have increased the known size of the mineralized envelopes of several deposits
and the Company expects to increase its total gold reserves and resources at
the end of this year, over and above the amount mined during the year.&#160; The Company&#146;s $54 million 2009 exploration
program is expected to result in approximately 221 kilometres of drilling using
more than 35 rigs.&#160; Close to 190
kilometres of exploration drilling have been completed through July, which is
almost 85% of the 2009 program.&#160; However,
based on the success of the program to date, it is expected that additional
expenditures will be authorized and the exploration programs expanded.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Highlights of the 2009 exploration program include:</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 45.0pt;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Symbol" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">At Pinos Altos:</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 81.0pt;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Symbol" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">New gold/silver zone discovered
at Cubiro</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 81.0pt;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Symbol" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Sinter zone&#146;s
better-than-expected grade and thickness suggest open pit potential</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 81.0pt;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Symbol" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">San Eligio zone extended
laterally and at depth</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 81.0pt;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 45.0pt;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Symbol" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">At Kittila:</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 81.0pt;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Symbol" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Deep drilling continued to
confirm strong grades at depths below 600 metres at Suuri and expanded the
underground resource envelope further to the north</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 81.0pt;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Symbol" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Near-surface gold
mineralization extended further north and at depth at Rimpi</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 45.0pt;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Symbol" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 45.0pt;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Symbol" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">At Meadowbank:</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 81.0pt;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Symbol" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Drilling results confirmed
mineralization extensions and underground mining potential of the Goose South
zone at depth</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 81.0pt;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Symbol" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">In-fill drilling also confirmed
the resource at Vault and extended the gold mineralization further north and
east</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 81.0pt;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;The ongoing extension
of known gold zones at several deposits and the discovery of the new gold zone
at Cubiro on the Pinos Altos property continue to demonstrate our ability to
expand our reserve base through exploration,&#148; said Sean Boyd, Vice-Chairman and
CEO. &#147;We expect this large and growing reserve base to be the foundation for</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">continued expansion in
gold production beyond 2010, as we complete several expansion studies at our recently
constructed gold mines,&#148; added Mr.&nbsp;Boyd.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Pinos
Altos Exploration Update &#151; Several Satellite Gold/Silver Deposits Taking Shape</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">At
the Pinos Altos project in Mexico, over 39 kilometres of drilling in a total of
139 drill holes was completed by the end of July, focusing on three new
mineralized structures.&#160; The first drill
program began in the spring on the newly discovered Cubiro zone and several
drill holes returned encouraging results.&#160;
This zone is located </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">approximately 10 kilometres northwest of Agnico-Eagle&#146;s
main Santo Nino pit.&#160; It is also
approximately two kilometres west of the Company&#146;s new Creston Mascota project,
where construction of an open pit, heap leach mine will begin in the fourth
quarter of 2009</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
infill program at Sinter, a parallel zone approximately two kilometres to the
north of the Santo Nino pit, is demonstrating a better average grade and
thickness than anticipated and may result in the development of a new satellite
open pit similar to Creston Mascota.&#160; At
San Eligio, another parallel zone less than one kilometre north of Santo Nino,
the drilling program extended the mineralization at depth and along strike to
the east and west.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/PinosLocationGeology_Sep09.pdf</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">New
Gold Discovery at Cubiro</font></i></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">T</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">he Cubiro mineralization is well exposed along the flanks of
the Conche&#241;o valley and is similar to the other deposits on the Pinos Altos
property.&#160; These deposits tend to be
quartz-calcite breccia vein systems with associated vein stockworks carrying
gold and silver.&#160; The Cubiro
mineralization was discovered in several showings in the valley and in shallow
historic workings that have been excavated along the most easterly vein
outcrops.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/CubiroPlanLongCross_Sep09.pdf</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The northwest-striking,
sub-vertical Cubiro mineralization forms an outcropping ridge, and has been
followed along strike for approximately 850 metres.&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Agnico-Eagle began to drill at the western part of the
new Cubiro zone in May&nbsp;2009.&#160; To the
end of July, a portable rig had drilled 3,600 metres in 19 holes.&#160; The best results were from two holes with
visible gold, CB-09-009 and CB-09-015.&#160;
CB-09-015 had two substantial intersections: 26 metres (all
intersections are estimated true width) grading 2.4 grams per tonne (&#147;g/t&#148;)
gold and 24.8 g/t silver, and 30 metres grading 4.4 g/t gold and 25.4 g/t
silver.&#160; Hole CB-09-009 returned 16.9
metres grading 2.3 g/t gold and 17.5 g/t silver.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The deposit remains open in all directions. </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;Road construction is underway and will provide
better access to the Cubiro deposit, where two rigs are currently drilling.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2</font></p>

<div style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Open Pit
Potential At Sinter</font></i></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Sinter zone is associated with the Reyna de Plata gold structure, located 1.7
kilometres north of the main Santo Nino pit.&#160;
The sub-vertical mineralization has been followed along strike for
almost 900 metres over a vertical depth of 350 metres and an estimated true
width between 4 and 35 metres. The deposit remains open along strike and at
depth.&#160; Agnico-Eagle&#146;s recent infill
drilling has indicated that the Sinter zone could become a satellite, heap
leach, low-grade, open pit deposit, similar to Creston Mascota.&#160; The best intersections to date have been hole
SIN-09-011, where 17.6 metres graded 3.3 g/t gold and 30.6 g/t silver, and hole
SIN-09-024, where 17.8 metres graded 2.4 g/t gold and 39.7 g/t silver.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/SinterLongCross_Sep09.pdf</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">With
the aid of the new access road, built to allow completion of the infill drill
program, a resource estimate is expected to be completed by the end of 2009.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Sinter
drill results</font></b></p>

  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.5%;">
  <p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="11%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:11.0%;">
  <p align="right" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">35.0</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.5%;">
  <p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="10%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:10.0%;">
  <p align="right" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.11</font></p>

  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.5%;">

  <td width="1%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.0%;">

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Mineralization
Extended At San Eligio</font></i></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The infill drilling program that began last
year at the San Eligio zone which is part of the main Pinos Altos mine deposit
continues to reveal a promising, steeply dipping zone of gold and silver
mineralization that is open laterally and at depth.&#160; An initial reserve was estimated in 2008 for
San Eligio, which included a combination of open pit and</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3</font></p>

<div style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='3',FILE='C:\JMS\105933\09-25836-1\task3713700\25836-1-ka-01.htm',USER='105933',CD='Sep 10 05:21 2009' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">underground mining, with probable reserves of
1.4 million tonnes grading 2.6 g/t gold and 115 g/t silver, containing 118,000
ounces of gold and 5.2 million ounces of silver.&#160; The highlights of the 2009 infill drill program
are two high-grade intersections on the east side of the current reserves.&#160; Hole PA-09-333 yielded 4.8 metres grading
24.3 g/t gold and 284.9 g/t silver above the current reserve area. One hundred
metres further east of the reserve outline, hole PA-09-362 yielded 3.5 metres
grading 4.3 g/t gold and 168 g/t silver.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In the western portion of the deposit,
drilling has also filled in gaps, with hole PA-09-357 returning 5.5 metres
grading 3.8 g/t gold and 162.0 g/t silver.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Deep exploration drilling outside and to the
west of the current resource envelope returned some significant
intercepts.&#160; In particular, hole
PA-09-354 yielded 4.0 metres grading 2.5 g/t gold and 120.0 g/t silver almost
200 metres below the current resource envelope.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">At year end, a new reserve and resource
estimate will be completed for San Eligio and it is expected that this zone
will be incorporated into the overall mining plan and the current production
expansion study at Pinos Altos.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/SanEligioLongCross_Sep09.pdf</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The table of drill highlights for San Eligio
follows:</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left"></div>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">*uncut</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Kittila Exploration Update &#151; Deep Drilling
Confirms Expansion Potential</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/KittilaLocation_Sep09.pdf</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The mineralization at the Kittila mine in
northern Finland continues to grow rapidly.&#160;
Kittila has significant potential for further resource to reserve
conversion, as well as the potential to extend the known envelope of
mineralization, especially below the Suuri and Roura deposits. Consequently,
almost 40% of Agnico-Eagle&#146;s drilling program in 2009 has been focused on
Kittila and other sites in Finland.&#160; To
date, 56 kilometres of the planned 86 kilometres have been drilled on the
Kittila mine site using 11 rigs.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/KittilaPlanLongCross_Sep09.pdf</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4</font></p>

<div style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='4',FILE='C:\JMS\105933\09-25836-1\task3713700\25836-1-ka-01.htm',USER='105933',CD='Sep 10 05:21 2009' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Suuri Zone</font></i></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Open pit mining at the main Suuri zone is
already underway and a ramp is being constructed to allow underground mining to
begin in 2010.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A study is currently underway regarding the
possibility of significantly expanding the operations.&#160; To access the deeper ore would require
sinking a mine shaft into the Suuri and adjacent Roura zones and expanding the
processing plant.&#160; To this end, six
drills are currently testing Suuri and Roura at depth. The study is expected to
be completed in the fourth quarter of 2009 and final review in the first
quarter of 2010.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Three horizons have been outlined at depth in
the Suuri Zone:&#160; East, Central and
West.&#160; Most of the drilling has been in
the East lens, with the resource-to-reserve conversion drilling this year
focused below the existing reserve (i.e., at depths below 600 metres).&#160; Results have confirmed the continuity of
grades and thicknesses previously reported for this lens.&#160; Significant results include hole SUU-09-005B,
which intersected 14.7 metres grading 7.14 g/t gold, and hole SUU-09-004, which
intersected 7.6 metres grading 8.32 g/t.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Some intercepts have confirmed the persistence
of the Suuri Zone&#146;s Central lens, such as hole SUU-08-003C, which had a
3.4-metre intercept grading 5.41 g/t gold. Similarly, hole SUU-08-001F returned
two intervals corresponding to the Central lens at depth, which returned 3.5
g/t gold over 6.0 metres and 8.6 g/t over almost 10 metres.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Some of the most encouraging drill results to
date, were on the northern edge of the Suuri Zone at depth, where it plunges
beneath the Roura Zone.&#160; Hole ROU-08-005
had two intersections in the East lens and a third believed to be in the
Central lens of the Suuri Zone.&#160; This is
regarded as especially encouraging because it is outside the present resource
model being considered for the Kittila production expansion study and deep underground
reserve project.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Suuri Deep Extensions drill results</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='5',FILE='C:\JMS\105933\09-25836-1\task3713700\25836-1-ka-01.htm',USER='105933',CD='Sep 10 05:21 2009' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Rimpi Zone</font></i></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A secondary objective of the 2009 drilling
program was to extend the Kittila deposit northward from Rimpi (located
adjacent to the Roura zone to the north).&#160;
The specific goals were to convert the inferred resources at Rimpi to
reserves, as well as to determine the extent of the mineralization.&#160; Results to date have been encouraging, as
drilling has confirmed the grades and thicknesses in this area, generally
ranging between 3 g/t to 5 g/t gold over 7 metres or more.&#160; Some of the best results were at depth, with
hole RCON-08-103 intersecting 5.5 metres grading 11.0 g/t gold.&#160; Mineralization was also found in two holes on
the northern limit of drilling, RIM-09-029 and RIM-09-032.&#160; The mineralization remains open to the north
at surface and shallowly plunges northward.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Several zones at Kittila remain open at depth
and along strike, particularly in the Suuri Deep and Rimpi areas. Successful
conversion drilling in these areas should have a positive effect on the economics
of the current expansion study.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Rimpi drill results</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Meadowbank Exploration Update &#151; Mineralization
Continues To Be Encountered Below Open Pit Reserves And Resources</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Exploration activities at Meadowbank in 2009
were focused on mine site exploration adjacent to the main Portage and Goose
Island gold deposits, regional exploration along the Meadowbank Trend (which
hosts the bulk of the current gold reserves and resources), and also along the
Northwest Trend (which hosts the PDF deposit). Results from this program will
be incorporated into the expansion study currently underway.&#160; To date, over 54 kilometres of drilling have
been completed and up to seven diamond drills have been active at Meadowbank.&#160; Some of the results are still pending.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/MeadowbankGeology_Sep09.pdf</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Meadowbank Minesite</font></i></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Minesite exploration in 2009 (over 27,400
metres in 100 holes using four diamond drills) has focused on testing for near
surface extensions to the current open pit reserves (particularly in the Goose
Island area), converting resource to potential underground reserves at Goose
South and testing for resource extensions along the Meadowbank mine trend
southward.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Goose
Island Open Pit Deposit Possibly Extended Southward</font></i></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Near
surface exploration immediately south of the Goose Island open pit deposit may
result in a further expansion of the open pit reserve in this area.&#160; Results received to </font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6</font></p>

<div style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">date
from the 23 drill hole (4,114 metre) campaign in 2009 suggest several
potentially economic gold intersections.&#160;
A cluster of holes (G-09-77, G-09-81 and G-09-87) returned gold values
of up to 5.6 g/t over 6.8 metres from an area that is relatively close to
surface and within 100 metres south of the currently planned Goose Island open
pit.&#160; Upon receipt of pending results
from several holes, the available information will be compiled in a review of
the Goose Island open pit zone.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/MeadowbankLongGooseCross_Sep09.pdf</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Goose
South Underground Zone potential</font></i></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Drilling
in the Goose South area, located immediately south of, and below, the Goose
Island open pit reserve has been focused on converting inferred resources into
reserves for a contemplated underground mine.&#160;
A total of 24 holes (11,038 metres) were drilled, primarily concentrated
at depths between 150 and 500 metres over a 1.2 kilometre stretch.&#160; The drilling was highly successful and
appears to have defined a higher grade core, which is roughly 500 metres long
and almost 300 metres deep (down to 500 metres).&#160; The zone is still open at depth to the north
and south.&#160; Some of the better intercepts
include hole G-09-20, which included 8.3 g/t gold over 5.0 metres at a depth of
approximately 200 metres and hole G-09-11, which included 8.9 g/t gold over 3.0
metres almost 540 metres below surface.&#160;
The results of this portion of the program will be included in a review
of the underground mining potential of the Goose South zone and will be
incorporated into the Meadowbank expansion study.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Gosling
Zone extended</font></i></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Gosling Zone lies roughly 400 metres south of the Goose Island open pit.&#160; This year&#146;s drilling campaign followed up
previous results that traced a near-surface occurrence over a length of
approximately 200 metres.&#160; Several holes
were drilled in 2009, which confirmed and extended the mineralization horizon
more than 100 metres deeper than previously known, and towards the south. Some
of the best results include 11.7 g/t over 2.8 metres in hole G09-54, located
almost at surface and 2.7 g/t over 8.9 metres in hole G09-57 at a depth of
approximately 75 metres below surface.&#160;
The zone is open at depth and to the south.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Meadowbank minesite drill results</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Regional Exploration</font></i></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The main target areas for regional exploration in 2009 were the
Meadowbank Trend (mainly southward from the mine site, but also northward in
the Vault deposit area) and the Northeast gold trend that crosses the property
in the vicinity of the PDF deposit.&#160; By
the end of July, almost 27 km (127 drill holes) were drilled by up to four
machines working during the winter-spring access on the Meadowbank
property.&#160; Since early June, exploration
has consisted of regional helicopter-supported geophysics, prospecting and
geologic mapping and diamond drilling using two rigs.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Meadowbank
Trend &#151; Developing South of the Minesite</font></i></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Exploration along the Meadowbank Trend to the south had an objective of
testing the south extension of the trend down to a depth of 200 metres.&#160; Several holes on sections south of the
Gosling zone returned significant results.&#160;
Drill hole GS-09-832 returned 3.1 g/t gold over 5.8 metres (including
4.1 g/t gold over 3.6 metres), and hole GS-09-834 returned 6.2 g/t gold over
4.4 metres (including 18 g/t gold over 1.4 metres).&#160; The intersections occurred at depths of 100 to
200 metres below previous holes, which had negligible results.&#160; Coupled with the Gosling results, these
results suggest the existence of significant gold mineralization with open pit
and underground potential along the Meadowbank trend south of the
minesite.&#160; This opens up exploration
potential not only southward but also northward at depth below the Goose Island
pit zone.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Future exploration, possibly from an underground ramp at Goose South will
likely target these new sectors of gold potential.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Meadowbank Trend South drill results</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

  <p align="right" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">226.9</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Estimated
true width is 75% of core length.</font></i></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Vault Deposit May&nbsp;Expand</font></i></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">At Vault, over 10 kilometres of drilling was
completed over 35 drill holes, with the objective of completing the conversion
of inferred resources within and immediately</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8</font></p>

<div style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">adjacent to the current pit design, as well as
testing for further extensions to the mineralization.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Results from inside current pit shell</font></i></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The resource to reserve conversion drilling was
successful in confirming continuity and grade in and immediately around the
current Vault pit shell and will likely convert inferred resources into
reserves.&#160; Drill hole VLT-09-287 returned
a broad interval of 1.73 g/t gold over 55 metres, including 7.3 g/t gold over
3.0 metres.&#160; Drill hole VLT-09-288A
returned two significant intervals of 3.15 g/t gold over 11.1 metres and 1.67
g/t gold over 27.0 metres, while drill hole VLT-09-292 returned 2.59 g/t gold
over 5.5 metres.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/VaultPlanCross_Sep09.pdf</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Results from outside current pit shell</font></i></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Twenty-five additional drill holes were
completed under the pit shell in order to extend the resource envelope and to
convert inferred resources into indicated resources.&#160; While some results are still pending, the
most significant results to date were holes VLT-09-275, VLT-09-284A and
VLT-09-295.&#160; Hole VLT-09-275 yielded 7.9
g/t gold over 6.6 metres within an envelope of almost 92 metres grading 1.1
g/t.&#160; Similarly, hole VLT-09-284A
returned a relatively thick 34.3 metres interval of 2.5 g/t gold including a
higher grade interval of 9.8 g/t gold over 3.6 metres.&#160; Hole VLT-09-295 yielded a similar higher
grade interval of 4.7 g/t gold over 7.5 metres, including 6.2 g/t gold over 5.2
metres.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Several other holes were drilled outside of the current resource
envelope for the purpose of extending the zone at depth and along strike.&#160; The deepest hole (VLT09-303) returned 2.2 g/t
gold over 6.0 metres. The most significant was hole VLT09-308, which returned
3.1 g/t gold over 28.5 metres, including a higher grade interval of 10.1 g/t
gold over 4.5 metres, indicating that the zone is still open at depth and to
the north.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Vault
South Beginning To Take Shape</font></i></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Vault South was one of the most significant discoveries made at
Meadowbank in 2008.&#160; The new zone has a
style of gold mineralization similar to Vault, but lies about one kilometre to
the southeast.&#160; Eight new drill holes
(1,724 metres) have been completed in 2009 on the Vault South target.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Drill hole VLTS-09-306, completed 50 metres south of the discovery hole
(VLT-08-273 returned 2.6 g/t gold over 4.1 metres), intersected 1.0 g/t gold
over 13 metres, including 2.4 g/t gold over 3.0 metres.&#160; Hole VLTS-09-309, completed to the west of
the discovery hole, intersected 0.9 g/t gold over 22.0 metres, including 2.4
g/t gold over 6.3 metres.&#160; The initial
results suggest that the mineralization is weaker towards the north.&#160; Results for holes VLTS-09-313 through
VLTS-09-317 are pending.&#160; Future
exploration in this area is warranted to further define this occurrence.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">About Agnico-Eagle</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Agnico-Eagle is
a long established Canadian gold producer with operations located in Quebec,
Finland and Mexico and exploration and development activities in Canada,
Finland, Mexico and the United States.&#160;
Agnico-Eagle&#146;s LaRonde mine is Canada&#146;s </font><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;</font><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">largest operating gold mine in terms of
reserves.&#160; The Company has full exposure
to higher gold prices consistent with its policy of no forward gold sales.&#160; It has declared a </font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Notes To Investors
Regarding The Use Of Resources</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cautionary Note To
Investors Concerning Estimates Of Measured And Indicated Resources</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This press
release uses the terms &#147;measured resources&#148; and &#147;indicated resources&#148;. We
advise investors that while those terms are recognized and required by Canadian
regulations, the SEC does not recognize them. <b>Investors
are cautioned not to assume that any part or all of mineral deposits in these
categories will ever be converted into reserves</b>.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cautionary Note To
Investors Concerning Estimates Of Inferred Resources</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This press
release also uses the term &#147;inferred resources&#148;. We advise investors that while
this term is recognized and required by Canadian regulations, the SEC does not
recognize it. &#147;Inferred resources&#148; have a great amount of uncertainty as to
their existence, and great uncertainty as to their economic and legal
feasibility. It cannot be assumed that all or any part of an inferred mineral
resource will ever be upgraded to a higher category. Under Canadian rules,
estimates of inferred mineral resources may not form the basis of feasibility
or pre-feasibility studies, except in rare cases. <b>Investors are cautioned not to assume that part or all of an inferred
resource exists, or is economically or legally mineable.</b></font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Scientific And Technical
Data</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Agnico-Eagle
Mines Limited is reporting mineral resource and reserve estimates in accordance
with the CIM guidelines for the estimation, classification and reporting of
resources and reserves.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cautionary Note To U.S.
Investors</font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">  <b>-</b> The
SEC permits U.S. mining companies, in their filings with the SEC, to disclose
only those mineral deposits that a company can economically and legally extract
or produce. We use certain terms in this press release, such as &#147;measured&#148;, &#147;indicated&#148;,
and &#147;inferred&#148;, and &#147;resources&#148; that the SEC guidelines strictly prohibit U.S.
registered companies from including in their filings with the SEC. U.S.
Investors are urged to consider closely the disclosure in our Form&nbsp;20-F,
which may </font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">15</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">be obtained
from us, or from the SEC&#146;s website at: </font><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">http://sec.gov/edgar.shtml.&#160; A &#147;final&#148;
or &#147;bankable&#148; feasibility study is required to meet the requirements to
designate reserves under Industry Guide 7.&#160;
Estimates were calculated using historic three-year average metals
prices and foreign exchange rates in accordance with the SEC Industry Guide
7.&#160; Industry Guide 7 requires the use of
prices that reflect current economic conditions at the time of reserve
determination which Staff of the SEC has interpreted to mean historic
three-year average prices.&#160; The
assumptions used for the mineral reserves and resources estimate reported by
the Company on February&nbsp;18th, 2009 were based on three-year average prices
for the period ending December&nbsp;31, 2008 of $725 per ounce gold, $13.32 per
ounce silver, $1.27 per pound zinc, $3.15 per pound copper, $0.90 per pound
lead and C$/US$, US$/Euro and MXP/US$ exchange rates of 1.09, 1.37 and 11.00,
respectively.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Canadian
Securities Administrators&#146; National Instrument 43-101 (&#147;NI 43-101&#148;) requires
mining companies to disclose reserves and resources using the subcategories of &#147;proven&#148;
reserves, &#147;probable&#148; reserves, &#147;measured&#148; resources, &#147;indicated&#148; resources and &#147;inferred&#148;
resources. Mineral resources that are not mineral reserves do not have
demonstrated economic viability.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A mineral
reserve is the economically mineable part of a measured or indicated resource
demonstrated by at least a preliminary feasibility study. This study must
include adequate information on mining, processing, metallurgical, economic and
other relevant factors that demonstrate, at the time of reporting, that
economic extraction can be justified. A mineral reserve includes diluting
materials and allows for losses that may occur when the material is mined. A
proven mineral reserve is the economically mineable part of a measured resource
for which quantity, grade or quality, densities, shape and physical
characteristics are so well established that they can be estimated with
confidence sufficient to allow the appropriate application of technical and
economic parameters, to support production planning and evaluation of the
economic viability of the deposit. A probable mineral reserve is the
economically mineable part of an indicated mineral resource for which quantity,
grade or quality, densities, shape and physical characteristics can be
estimated with a level of confidence sufficient to allow the appropriate
application of technical and economic parameters, to support mine planning and
evaluation of the economic viability of the deposit.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A mineral
resource is a concentration or occurrence of natural, solid, inorganic or
fossilized organic material in or on the Earth&#146;s crust in such form and
quantity and of such a grade or quality that it has reasonable prospects for
economic extraction. The location, quantity, grade, geological characteristics
and continuity of a mineral resource are known, estimated or interpreted from
specific geological evidence and knowledge. A measured mineral resource is that
part of a mineral resource for which quantity, grade or quality, densities,
shape and physical characteristics can be estimated with a level of confidence
sufficient to allow the appropriate application of technical and economic
parameters, to support mine planning and evaluation of the economic viability
of the deposit. The estimate is based on detailed and reliable exploration,
sampling and testing information gathered through appropriate techniques from
locations such as outcrops, trenches, pits, workings and drill holes that are
spaced closely enough to confirm both geological and grade continuity. An
indicated mineral resource is that part </font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">16</font></p>

<div align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">of a mineral
resource for which quantity, grade or quality, densities, shape and physical
characteristics can be estimated with a level of confidence sufficient to allow
the appropriate application of technical and economic parameters, to support
mine planning and evaluation of the economic viability of the deposit. The
estimate is based on detailed and reliable exploration and testing information
gathered through appropriate techniques from locations such as outcrops,
trenches, pits, workings and drill holes that are spaced closely enough for
geological and grade continuity to be reasonably assumed. An inferred mineral
resource is that part of a mineral resource for which quantity and grade or
quality can be estimated on the basis of geological evidence and limited
sampling and reasonably assumed, but not verified, geological and grade
continuity. The estimate is based on limited information and sampling gathered
through appropriate techniques from locations such as outcrops, trenches, pits,
workings and drill holes. Mineral resources which are not mineral reserves do
not have demonstrated economic viability.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Investors are cautioned
not to assume that part or all of an inferred resource exists, or is
economically or legally mineable.</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A feasibility
study is a comprehensive study of a mineral deposit in which all geological,
engineering, legal, operating, economic, social, environmental and other
relevant factors are considered in sufficient detail that it could reasonably
serve as the basis for a final decision by a financial institution to finance
the development of the deposit for mineral production.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The mineral
reserves presented in this disclosure are separate from and not a portion of
the mineral resources.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
